## Replication checklist

1. Load or map the 4 captured computed font stacks, in priority order: <code>NeueMontreal, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif</code>, <code>HWCigars, Georgia, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif</code>, <code>ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Symbol&quot;, &quot;Noto Color Emoji&quot;</code>, <code>Inter-Variable, Helvetica, sans-serif</code>. Reproduce every size, weight, line-height, letter-spacing, and style variant from the typography tables.

2. Define tokens for all 58 captured colors using the hex and role evidence above. Preserve alpha channels and use occurrence counts only for prioritization, not as pixel-area estimates.

3. Implement the spacing system from 52 common values, 9 container widths, 7 radii, and 1 shadows; then encode every captured breakpoint condition.

4. Build the 17 outline sections in the exact numbered order from the layout chapter: 1) header, 2) nav, 3) hero, 4) main, 5) section, 6) section, 7) section, 8) section, 9) section, 10) section, 11) section, 12) section, 13) section, 14) section, 15) section, 16) section, 17) section. Match each section’s dimensions, structure counts, and computed-style block before adding minor content.

5. Apply all 17 section background records, then recreate 14 captured video/canvas hero media and 124 inline SVG records from the effects chapter.

6.
